 ) The historic and oldest temple of Jageshwar Mahadev, witnessing the beginning of Shivalinga Puja in the world, is still looking forward to recognition of its grandeur and fame
 uttarakhand ke almoda jile ke mukhyalay se kareeb 40 kilometre dur deodaar ke vrikshon ke ghaney jangalon ke bich pahari par sthit jageshwar mahadev ke mandir parisar main parvati, hanuman, mrityunjay mahadev, bhairav, kedarnath, durga sahit kul 124 mandir sthit hai jinamein aaj bhi vidhiwat puja hoti he
 The chief priest of the temple, Shashti Dutt Bhatt, told the language correspondent in a special conversation that the Archaeological Department of India has named this temple as one of the two Jyotirlingas of the country and has also installed a stone slab announcing it
 ek sachaai yah bhi he ki isi mandir se hi bhagwaan shiv kii ling puja ke rup main shuruuaat hui thi
 It was only after worship here that Shivalinga started to be worshiped all over the world and many self-made Shivalingas later came to be worshiped as Jyotirlinga

 dutt ne bataaya ki duniya main bhagwaan shiv kii ling ke rup main puja kii shuruuaat isi mandir se hui thi or iskaa zikr shivpurana ke maanas khand main hua he

 unhone kaha ki mandir kii pracheenta sabit karne vaale board ko phir se lagaaya janaa chaiye
 He said that the Chandala kings had saved this temple and later the Katyuri kings also donated many villages to the Jageshwar temple, which used to arrange the worship of the temple
